婕伊：任务蓝图补充 - Jae_Q1（2/3）

返回角色目录 | 返回同伴目录

场景：Queue

  • 注：出现条件：Quest

队伍之中，成千上万人的声音在嗡嗡作响。有的人铺好了被褥，已经安然入睡，有的人在演奏某种古怪的乐器，还有许多人在祈祷。此外，还有几位来自贵族阶层的请愿者，不停地争论着谁的事务最重要。
The queue hums with thousands of voices. Someone has rolled out bedding and is settling down to sleep; someone is playing some bizarre musical instrument; many are praying. Several highborn petitioners are debating who is here on the most important business.

“不得不承认，帝国宏伟的行政机器也同样有着欠缺打磨的边缘……”婕伊腼腆地笑了笑，注视着排队的人。“不过，这可真是场激动人心的冒险，亲爱的！我以前从来没见过这样的场面……有的时候，从旅途中停歇下来，休息一下，也很不错。这样一来，那些血气方刚的新人也可以沐浴在属于他们自己的荣光之下，不会再因为我们而黯然失色。”
"You have to admit, the magnificent administrative machinery of the Imperium isn't without its rough edges..." Jae smiles sheepishly, eying the queue. "But what a thrilling adventure this is turning out to be, shereen! I've never seen anything like it before... And sometimes it's good to take a break from constant travelling. And to give all the hot-blooded newcomers a chance to cover themselves in glory without us in the way."

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

[打个呵欠]
[Yawn]

时间拖得很慢，让人难以忍受。在队伍的某处，有个孩子在大哭大叫。大厅中的文员们正不紧不慢地把一堆文件挪到另一堆，纸张在文件堆之间不断穿梭。有几位请愿者正聚在一起，扯些有的没的，还有的人躺在附近的长椅上打着盹。
The minutes drag by intolerably slowly. Somewhere in the queue, a child is howling at the top of its lungs, the palace adepts are sedately moving documents from one pile to another, shuffling papers. Several petitioners have gathered in a huddle and are swapping rumours, while someone has laid down for a nap on a nearby bench.

  • 选择 Choice

[挠挠脖子]
[Scratch the back of your neck]

你成功地打发掉了三十秒等待的时间，你很想知道还要再等多长时间。
You have whiled away thirty seconds of your wait. You wonder how long you have left to go.

  • 选择 Choice

[数一下有多少人在排队]
[Count the people in the queue]

人们不断地移动着，来来去去。有些人换了地方，还有些人直接从你的视野中消失了。在你第一次尝试数的时候，你数到了238个人，第二次的时候，你数到了244个人。而当你第三次尝试的时候，一批不幸的请愿者被送进了大厅，于是你忘记自己数到多少了。
The people are constantly moving, coming and going, changing places or simply disappearing from view. On your first attempt, you count two hundred and thirty-eight petitioners. On your second attempt, you count two hundred and forty-four. On your third attempt, the next batch of unlucky souls is ushered into the hall, and you lose count.

  • 注：出现条件：Companion

“老实说……”婕伊留意到你的目光之后，她一边盯着绮贝菈，一边嘀嘀咕咕地开了口。“亲爱的，如果你能让你的宠物刺客在这里进行一场小小表演的话……我敢说排队的人肯定会少很多。”
"Actually..." After catching your eye, Jae purrs surreptitiously as she glances at Kibellah, "Shereen, if you were to tell your pet assassin to put on a little show in this room right now... I bet the queue would get a lot shorter."

“你打算玷污织血罗网的圣礼，用来满足你的贪婪？再好好想想吧，亵渎者。”
"To defile one of the Bloodspun Web's sacraments by dedicating it to your avarice? Think again, blasphemer."

  • 选择 Choice

[命令你的仆人准备一块符合行商浪人身份的等待区]
[Order your servants to prepare a waiting area befitting a Rogue Trader]

你感觉到其他请愿者以艳羡的目光注视着你，但那些人只是盯着你看，谁都不敢轻举妄动。
You feel the envious eyes of the other petitioners upon you, but no one dares to do anything more than stare.

  • 选择 Choice

[耐心等待]
[Wait patiently]

在过去的八个小时里，等待大厅中唯一的变化就是守卫换了班。队伍中的请愿者平静地等待着至福的时刻，等待他们的请愿被帝国的高级官员受理。突然，一个声音响了起来，整个队列的人变得兴奋不已。“285号，请前往审理窗口。”
In the last eight hours, the only thing that has changed in the waiting hall is the warden shift. The petitioners in the queue placidly await the blessed hour when their appeal will be heard by the high-ranking servants of the Imperium. The entire queue perks up at a sudden announcement: "Number 285, proceed to the available window."

“让黄金王座带走我吧，这到底是什么样的折磨啊？”婕伊几乎发出了绝望的哀嚎。“我们浪费了这么多宝贵的时间，却仅仅前进了三个位置。恐怕还没等咱们排完队，咱们就要变得老态龙钟了，亲爱的。”
"Throne take me, what torturous trial have we let ourselves in for?" Jae almost wails in despair. "So much precious time lost, and we've only moved three places ahead! At this rate, we'll be old and grey before we get out of this queue, shereen."

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice
  • 注：显示条件：有条件

[耐心等待]“要恪守信念，姐妹。只有保持耐心与谦卑，才能得到真正的智慧。”
[Wait patiently] "Gird your faith, sister. For it is only through patience and humility that true wisdom comes."

“谦逊、恭良、温顺……我根本没有这些品质，亲爱的。”婕伊尖刻地笑着，不再打扰你的思考。
"Humility, acceptance, meekness... Those are the qualities that I entirely lack, shereen." Jae smiles acidly and leaves you alone with your thoughts.

又过了八个小时。队伍中的人几乎一动不动，而隔壁窗口的认证官则忙着处理沉思者中拒绝服从命令的机魂。因此，那个窗口的队伍也插进了你的队伍之中。
Another eight planetary hours go by. The queue has hardly moved — the adept in the next window was dealing with rebelling machine spirits in his cogitator, so the petitioners from that queue were diverted to the middle of yours.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

你在队伍中迎来了黄昏，又迎来了黎明。你通过大厅的窗户，观察着瓦兰修斯领不断变化的天光。夜晚平静地过去了，认证官离开了窗口，去睡觉了，机仆们替代了他们的位置。但遗憾的是，机仆并不能处理请愿者的所有请求。因此，到了晚上，队伍移动得更加缓慢。
You greeted the dusk and dawn from your place in the queue, observing the shifting rays of the Mundis Valancius through the windows of the palace. The night passed peacefully — the certification officers left for their beds and servitors took their place. Unfortunately, servitors cannot process all petitioner requests, so at night the queue moved even more slowly.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“居然把审判庭的宝贵时间浪费在这种愚蠢的事情上，这简直让人无法想象！”海因里希已经忍受不了漫长的等待，正在重读数据板上的机密报告。这已经是他第十次重读了。
"Wasting the Inquisition's time on this foolishness, it's simply unthinkable!" Wearied by the long wait, Heinrix is rereading confidential reports on his data-slate for the tenth time.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“又到了这个该死的地方。当我打算结婚的时候，就在这条队伍里等着。每当我的子女出生时，我都不得不在这条队伍里等着，这样他们的名字才会被记入达戈努斯的史册。而当我挚爱的妻子离世的时候，我依然在等着。”阿贝拉德垂头丧气地叹息着。
"This accursed place again. I stood in this queue when I was planning to marry. I stood in it when every son and every daughter was born, so that their names would be entered in the chronicle of Dargonus. And when my dear wife departed this mortal world, I waited again." Abelard sighs dejectedly.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“噢，舰长大人，这个地方充斥着褪了色的丑陋污点！我感到头晕目眩……”卡西娅用厚厚的披肩遮住了双眼。“事实证明，帝国内政部的殿堂就像那些仆人写出来的作品一样，令人失望不已。”
"Oh, Lord Captain, this place teems with hideous stains of washed-out colours! It makes my head spin..." Cassia covers her eyes with a thick shawl. "The Palace of the Adeptus Administratum has proved to be just as depressing as the published works of its servants."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

今天，整个首都都在庆祝你祖先的诞辰。当初，就是米尔蒂亚斯·奥勒斯特·希恩·冯·瓦兰修斯发现了基亚瓦伽马星，在那里建立了殖民地。达戈努斯的每座巢都都在举行祈祷仪式。贵族与平民涌上街头，参加各种娱乐活动，就连德莱夫斯塔总督本人都登上了宫殿的尖塔，发表了年度演讲。内政部绝大多数仆人都加入了这场庆典，因此，今天只有一位认证官在处理各种事务。
Today the entire capital is celebrating the birthday of your ancestor — Miltiades Orest Theon von Valancius, who discovered and colonised Kiava Gamma. In every hive on Dargonus, prayer services are being held in his honour, nobles and commoners are attending fairs with amusements, and Governor Drivestem himself is giving his annual speech from the main spire of his palace. Most of the Administratum servants have joined the festivities, so today all of the windows are being served by only one certification officer.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“正在记录毫无建设性，浪费时间资源的行为。建议解决方案：返回初始任务。”
"Unconstructive expenditure of temporal resources recorded. Recommended resolution: return to initial mission."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“混沌大敌正在整个科罗努斯扩区策划阴谋，准备对付神皇的追随者，可我们却不得不在这里等待一纸凭证！”阿洁塔愤怒地瞪着婕伊。“而且，这么做还不是为了帝国的利益，不是！而是为了满足某个异端分子的异想天开！”
"The Archenemy is plotting against His servants throughout the Expanse, and we are forced to wait here for a piece of paper to be certified!" Argenta tosses a furious look at Jae. "And not for the good of the Imperium, no, but to satisfy the whim of a heretic!"

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“舰长大人，这个地方实在是太无聊了，就连另一边的敲门声都没有了。那些家伙意识到这里没有任何有趣的事情，甚至都不再窃窃私语了！咱们就不能回到船上去吗？”
"Lord Captain, this place is so dull there's not even any knocking on the other side of the door — all the whispers died down when they realised nothing interesting was going to happen! Can't we go back to the ship?"

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

索罗蒙仿佛石像一样，面无表情地站在一大群卑微的请愿者之中，身躯一动不动，目光不停地扫视着周围。
Solomorne stands impassively like a stone column amidst the throng of lowly petitioners, unmoving except for his eyes, which sweep the perimeter like a guard-visor.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

接下来的八个小时，也同样是出乎意料地平静。没有发生任何不寻常的事情，所有的认证官都在各自的窗口接待请愿者。你甚至已经渐渐开始习惯这个地方的声音与气味了。
The next eight hours pass surprisingly peacefully — nothing unusual happens, all the certification officers are at their windows and are accepting petitioners, and you have even started growing accustomed to the sounds and smells of this place.

“亲爱的……你真是个圣人，我以前有没有这么说过？你绝对是个圣人，因为你的耐心是如此热忱，又是如此毫无意义，我根本看不出来你为什么要这么做。我们就不能抓紧时间吗？”
"Shereen... You're a saint, have I told you that before? You must be, because I don't see any other reason why you would show such fervent but senseless patience. Can't we hurry things along?"

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

队伍中再次散发出了充满活力的嗡嗡声。请愿者们互相打量着，握紧了各自的叫号票。几秒种后，你意识到，伺服头骨第三次喊出的号码，就是你的票上的号码。
The hum of activity returns to the queue. Petitioners exchange glances, clutching their paperwork. After a few seconds, you realise that the number being called out by the servo-skull for the third time is the one on your ticket.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

由于缺乏睡眠，过度劳累，加之喝了艾玛赛克酒，婕伊的眼睛凹进了眼窝。她的头发变得乱糟糟的，原本精美的衣服也变得皱皱巴巴，看起来就像是刚刚和谁打了一架。“我们……真的等到号了吗？我敢向黄金王座发誓，耐心简直是通往疯狂的道路。我真不敢想象，那些圣徒怎么能在没有艾玛赛克酒的情况下，忍受得了这样的折磨……”
Jae's eyes are sunken from lack of sleep, amasec, and exhaustion. Her hair is dishevelled, and her fine clothing is so rumpled one would think she had been brawling. "We've... really made it? I swear on the Throne, patience is the path to madness. I don't know how the saints live through their torments without amasec..."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

“噢，至高无上的神皇啊，感谢你赐予行商浪人神圣的授状与特权！我对天发誓，如果我们当时再多等一分钟，我肯定会开枪打人了！”
"O, Exalted One, thank you for granting the Rogue Trader his/her sacred Warrant and all its privileges! If we had had to wait a minute longer, heaven be my witness, I would have shot someone!"

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

“有些东西越是等待就越是美妙，你知道是什么吗，亲爱的？是艾玛赛克酒，还有交欢。如果我下次再让你排队的话，记得提醒我这件事情。”
"Do you know what gets better with time, shereen? Amasec and lovemaking. Remind me of that if I ever ask you to stand in a queue again."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

“嗯……这比我想象得要快。当然，我们确实等了一小会儿，不过有的时候，等待也是件有趣的事情。”婕伊疲惫地笑着。“只有再盖上最后一个印章，再认证一次……帝国官方贸易代表婕伊·海达利就会站在你面前了！”
"Well... That went faster than I expected. We had a little bit of a wait, of course, but at times it was actually fun." Jae smiles wearily. "One last seal. One more certification and... you will be looking at Official Trade Representative Jae Heydari!"

“还在等什么呢，亲爱的？赶紧走吧，咱们还要花上几个小时的时间，和认证官磨嘴皮子呢。”
"What are you waiting for, shereen? Let's go. We have another couple of hours with the certification officer to get through."

“好吧，亲爱的。或许你这次会失去耐心，打算让事情进行得快一些？”
"Well, shereen, maybe this time you will lose patience with being patient and decide to move things along a teensy bit faster?"

  • 选择 Choice

“我们得快点前进才行，用用你的小伎俩吧。”
"We need to move forward faster. Use your tricks."

  • 注：出现条件：有条件

“我更愿意称之为‘经年累月积累下来的智慧’……不过，随便怎么叫都好吧。你打算怎么做呢，亲爱的？”
"I'd prefer to call it my wisdom learned through many years' experience... But I don't care about the precise wording just now. How do you wish to proceed, shereen?"

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“咱们来解决一下这些平民百姓的问题吧。”
"We shall solve the problems of the common people."

“真是个明智的决定，亲爱的！冷市商人都是这么说的：如果问题可以靠钱解决，那花在这上面的钱，仅仅是做生意的成本而已！”
"A wise decision, shereen! Cold Traders always say: if you can solve a problem with hard cash, then that's just the cost of doing business!"

婕伊意有所指地看了你一眼，之后稍稍退了一步。“噢，至高无上的神皇在上，莫非今天是我的幸运日吗？我再也不用在这个大厅里日夜等候了，因为冯·瓦兰修斯家族这位善良的大人/女士是所有穷苦之人的庇护主，他/她已经帮我解决了我的问题！”
Jae gives you a conspiratorial wink and backs away slightly. "O Exalted One, could today be my lucky day? No longer will I have to stand in this hall, waiting day and night for my turn to come, for this kind lord/lady of House von Valancius is a benefactor of the downtrodden, and he/she has solved my problem!"

“尊敬的大人/女士，请您可怜可怜我这个年轻人吧！只要你能帮忙解决我的问题，我向帝皇发誓，我愿意把我的一切都献给您！”
"Esteemed lord/lady, take pity on this poor youth as well! I will give you everything I have, I swear before the Emperor! Only help me solve my problem."

“我们才不需要你献出一切呢，可怜虫。只要把你的位置让给我们就行了。”
"We do not need everything, poor wretch. Only your place in the queue."

“我将尽我所能。”

"Emperor grant me patience..."

合流：共同后续 / Rejoin: shared continuation

这个年轻人穿着破旧的工作服。虽然他只是一介平民，但他的举止却异常优雅。“大人，我已经在这个队列里等了二十四个月了。我希望能得到一张许可，让我与我的未婚妻萨姿结婚。可遗憾的是，如果得不到来自贵族担保人的签名，内政部的仆人就不肯批准许可……”
The young man in worn work overalls comports himself with unusual grace for a commoner. "My lord/lady, I have been in this queue for two dozen moons already, trying to get a permission slip to wed my fiancée Zazi. Unfortunately, the servants of the Administratum refuse to grant it without the signature of a highborn sponsor..."

“都给我让开！”一位衣着华丽的女士把左右的围观者推开，朝你冲了过来。她的嘴唇上面有颗美人痣。“尊贵的大人，我的第八个儿子发了疯！他打算放弃他的家庭地位、贵族头衔与身为治疗师的天赋，一门心思要和某个来自中产阶层的姑娘结婚！如果他真的与一介平民结了婚，就没办法继续完成大学的学业了。难道达戈努斯的医疗机构，真的要因为我儿子一时心血来潮，失去一位前途似锦的外科医师吗？”
"Out of my way!" Elbowing aside onlookers left and right, a richly dressed lady with a beauty mark augment above her lip charges toward you. "Esteemed lord/lady, my eighth offspring has lost his mind! He has decided to renounce his family, his noble title, and his talent as a healer, all for the sake of some tattered waif from the middle levels! A union with a commoner will put an end to his studies at the university — but should Dargonus and the Officio Medicae be deprived of a capable chirurgeon because of a passing fancy?"

“萨姿也同样是治疗师！她帮助过许多巢都民众，比那些拿着文凭的花哨医生救治的人要多得多！我可不想像你一样，一辈子活在达戈努斯的尖塔里，过着百无聊赖的人生。既然我已经知道，巢都底层有成百上千不幸的民众需要我来救助，那我就更不能这么做了！”
"Zazi is a healer too! And she helps the people of the hive a great deal more than any lily-white chirurgeon with a diploma! I do not want to live a life of idleness in the spires of Dargonus like you, not when I know there are thousands of unfortunate people in the lower levels who need my help!"

  • 选择 Choice

“我对你们的卿卿我我不感兴趣，但如果你需要担保人的话，我可以给你签个字。”
"I have no interest in your little drama. I will sign the paper if you require a sponsor."

“谢谢您，大人！我保证会将您的慷慨告知我的儿女，以及我的孙辈！”
"Thank you, my lord/lady! I promise I will tell my children and my children's children of your kindness!"

“你处理事务的方式很有趣，亲爱的。我会牢记这一点的。”婕伊目视着年轻的请愿者离开，精明的双眼中闪烁着饶有兴致的光芒。
"You have an interesting way of doing business, shereen. I'll keep that in mind." Jae's shrewd eyes are alight with interest as she watches the young petitioner leave.

在短暂的停顿之后，一位破衣烂衫的驼背老人朝你走了过来。这个老人的牙齿已经掉光。他张开口，呼出一团恶臭。断断续续地说了四个字：“重……获……新生……”
After allowing you a brief pause, a hunched ragamuffin approaches you. The old man's toothless mouth breathes out a putrefying cloud of air as he speaks only three words: "Death-th-th... f-f-for life..."

婕伊的目光越过了他的肩膀，看着他手上皱巴巴的表格。“你……是来请求进行遗体捐赠的吗？这样一来，你的器官就可以作为你的遗产，归你的孙女所有，对吗？但她恐怕不会想要你破破烂烂的身体，老家伙……”
Jae peers over the man's shoulder to read his crumpled form. "You... are here to request mortification, so that your organs go to your granddaughter as an inheritance? She will hardly want your worn-out body parts, old-timer..."

这个衣衫褴褛的人摇了摇头，满是皱纹的手遮住了他的脸。“机仆……配件！”
The ragged man shakes his head and covers his face with his wrinkled hands. "S-s-servitor... Disp-po-posal!"

  • 选择 Choice

“贱民的生命毫无价值。等你完成大学的学业之后，你才会有资格拯救那些真正有价值的人。”
"The lives of commoners hold no value. When you finish university, you will be qualified to save those who are truly worthy."

年轻人考虑几分钟之后，撕烂了手中的申请单。“您说得没错，把妓女与酒鬼从死亡的边缘拖回来，并不是什么光彩的事情。这么说来，自我堕落的贵族也同样没有拯救的价值。”他冷冷地看着他的母亲。“我生来就是为了拯救别人的生命。现在看来，恐怕没有比帝国卫队更适合我的地方了。”
The young man considers this for a few minutes, and then rips up his piece of paper. "You are right. There is no honour in dragging back trollops and drunks from the edge of death. Or self-indulgent nobles, for that matter." He looks coldly at his mother. "I was born to save lives. And there is no better place to do that than in the Imperial Guard."

“不，斯特福，我不是这个意思——住手！求求你了！好好考虑考虑吧！”
"No, Steffo, that's not what I— stop! Please! Think about this!"

“你处理事务的方式很有趣，亲爱的。我会牢记这一点的。”婕伊目视着年轻的请愿者离开，精明的双眼中闪烁着饶有兴致的光芒。
"You have an interesting way of doing business, shereen. I'll keep that in mind." Jae's shrewd eyes are alight with interest as she watches the young petitioner leave.

"If these ashmags want to be tricked, I won't stop them." Jae smugly watches the agitated crowd, whispering among themselves and jabbing each other with sheaves of paper.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

队伍中再次散发出了充满活力的嗡嗡声。请愿者们互相打量着，握紧了各自的叫号票。几秒种后，你意识到，伺服头骨第三次喊出的号码，就是你的票上的号码。
The hum of activity returns to the queue. Petitioners exchange glances, clutching their paperwork. After a few seconds, you realise that the number being called out by the servo-skull for the third time is the one on your ticket.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

"Do you know what gets better with time, shereen? Amasec and lovemaking. Remind me of that if I ever ask you to stand in a queue again."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

"Well... That went faster than I expected. We had a little bit of a wait, of course, but at times it was actually fun." Jae smiles wearily. "One last seal. One more certification and... you will be looking at Official Trade Representative Jae Heydari!"

  • 注：出现条件：有条件

[看着某个看起来心地善良的人]
[Address a tender-hearted man]

婕伊循着你的目光，将手搭在某个看起来很疲惫的人肩膀上。“愿帝皇照亮你的道路，兄弟！我是婕伊，这位是{name}。咱们一起排了这么久的队，甚至可以算得上是一家人了。可不可以告诉我们，是什么原因让你来到了这座秩序的殿堂？”
Jae catches your eye and lays her hand on the shoulder of a weary-looking man. "May the Emperor illuminate your path, brother! I am Jae, and this is {name}. We've been in the queue so long already, we're all practically family now — won't you tell us what brought you to the palace of order?"

那个男人惊讶地开了口。“呃？没错，没错，愿黄金王座的光芒保佑你！我叫梅纳斯，梅纳斯·德·皮尔。我已经在这里呆了一个月了，试遍了所有办法，想到达那扇窗户，但无论什么方法都不管用。我可怜的伊莲娜，我可怜的亲生女儿。那些人把她扣留在了维博斯六号星，还对她提出了指控，你敢相信会发生这种事情吗？那些指控都是假的！我们的内政部就是这么不干人事。”说完这句话，梅纳斯赶紧捂住了嘴，惊恐地四处张望。
The man starts in surprise. "Eh? Yes, yes, light of the Throne bless you! My name is Menas. Menas de Pyrr. I have been here a month already. I've tried everything I can to get through to that window. Nothing working. My poor, poor Ilena. She's my daughter, my flesh and blood. They detained her on Vheabos VI. Charged her — can you believe it? The charges were false! That's how our Administratum operates." Menas covers his mouth and glances around fearfully.

“我有点说过头了，我真的很抱歉。那都是在瞎说，瞎说而已。我只是在想我的女儿，她被关在维博斯，被铐在矿井里。我可怜的伊莲娜！她就像鲜花一样娇嫩。她的肺不好，你懂的吧？她总是咳嗽，可她现在却被关在了矿井里？要呼吸那么多灰尘和泥土？她受不了，她绝对受不了！她本该两年前就无罪释放了，可她依然被关在里面，就因为我没弄到认证和印章，你敢相信吗？这么长时间过去了……而我却站在这里，一直在等着。算了，这已经不重要了。总之，按照这个队伍现在的速度，恐怕我们至少要等上十个周期，才能等到叫号。”
"I've said too much. I do apologise — it's my nerves. My nerves. I just keep thinking about her there on Vheabos, shackled down in the mines. My poor, poor Ilena! As delicate as a flower, she is. She's got weak lungs, you understand? Always coughing. And her now down the mines? All that dust and muck? She won't cope with it, she won't! She was acquitted two years ago. But to get the papers certified, and the seal? So much time has passed... And now here I am, standing, waiting. It doesn't matter. At the rate this queue's moving, it'll be ten cycles or more before our numbers come up."

And the smugglers were found too. And what did the smugglers do? They framed someone else. And my daughter was charged!"

那个男人惊讶地开了口。“呃？没错，没错，愿黄金王座的光芒保佑你！我叫梅纳斯，梅纳斯·德·皮尔。我已经在这里呆了一个月了，试遍了所有办法，想到达那扇窗户，但无论什么方法都不管用。我可怜的伊莲娜，我可怜的亲生女儿。那些人把她扣留在了维博斯六号星，还对她提出了指控，你敢相信会发生这种事情吗？那些指控都是假的！我们的内政部就是这么不干人事。”说完这句话，梅纳斯赶紧捂住了嘴，惊恐地四处张望。
The man starts in surprise. "Eh? Yes, yes, light of the Throne bless you! My name is Menas. Menas de Pyrr. I have been here a month already. I've tried everything I can to get through to that window. Nothing working. My poor, poor Ilena. She's my daughter, my flesh and blood. They detained her on Vheabos VI. Charged her — can you believe it? The charges were false! That's how our Administratum operates." Menas covers his mouth and glances around fearfully.

“我有点说过头了，我真的很抱歉。那都是在瞎说，瞎说而已。我只是在想我的女儿，她被关在维博斯，被铐在矿井里。我可怜的伊莲娜！她就像鲜花一样娇嫩。她的肺不好，你懂的吧？她总是咳嗽，可她现在却被关在了矿井里？要呼吸那么多灰尘和泥土？她受不了，她绝对受不了！她本该两年前就无罪释放了，可她依然被关在里面，就因为我没弄到认证和印章，你敢相信吗？这么长时间过去了……而我却站在这里，一直在等着。算了，这已经不重要了。总之，按照这个队伍现在的速度，恐怕我们至少要等上十个周期，才能等到叫号。”
"I've said too much. I do apologise — it's my nerves. My nerves. I just keep thinking about her there on Vheabos, shackled down in the mines. My poor, poor Ilena! As delicate as a flower, she is. She's got weak lungs, you understand? Always coughing. And her now down the mines? All that dust and muck? She won't cope with it, she won't! She was acquitted two years ago. But to get the papers certified, and the seal? So much time has passed... And now here I am, standing, waiting. It doesn't matter. At the rate this queue's moving, it'll be ten cycles or more before our numbers come up."

“最简单的方法，就是让这些卑贱的臣民在我们尊贵的身份面前俯首称臣，亲爱的。至于第二个方法，则需要更多的……耐心。我已经找到了我们的第一位受害——呃，第一位富有同情心的公民，他比我们靠前50个人。只要说出正确的话语，解开他的心结，他就会很乐意和你换票。而且……你有能力解决一部分请愿者的问题，这样他们就不需要再去窗口进行请愿了。毕竟，你是群星的征服者，而他们只是普通民众，他们怎么可能会有你实现不了的愿望呢？”
"The simplest way is to make these lowly subjects bow down before the blinding radiance of our title, shereen. The second option requires a little more... patience. I have already found our first vict— ah, the compassionate citizen who is standing fifty places ahead of us in the queue. Simply offer the right words to unlock his heart and he will gladly swap tickets with you. And also... you have the power to solve the problems of some petitioners, removing their need to visit a coveted window. After all, is there anything an ordinary citizen could want that is beyond the power of the conqueror of the stars to grant?"

The young man in worn work overalls comports himself with unusual grace for a commoner. "Out of my way!" Elbowing aside onlookers left and right, a richly dressed lady with a beauty mark augment above her lip charges toward you. "Esteemed lord/lady, my eighth offspring has lost his mind! He has decided to renounce his family, his noble title, and his talent as a healer, all for the sake of some tattered waif from the middle levels! A union with a commoner will put an end to his studies at the university — but should Dargonus and the Officio Medicae be deprived of a capable chirurgeon because of a passing fancy?"

“萨姿也同样是治疗师！她帮助过许多巢都民众，比那些拿着文凭的花哨医生救治的人要多得多！我可不想像你一样，一辈子活在达戈努斯的尖塔里，过着百无聊赖的人生。既然我已经知道，巢都底层有成百上千不幸的民众需要我来救助，那我就更不能这么做了！”
"Zazi is a healer too! And she helps the people of the hive a great deal more than any lily-white chirurgeon with a diploma! I do not want to live a life of idleness in the spires of Dargonus like you, not when I know there are thousands of unfortunate people in the lower levels who need my help!"

这个衣衫褴褛的人摇了摇头，满是皱纹的手遮住了他的脸。“机仆……配件！”
The ragged man shakes his head and covers his face with his wrinkled hands. "S-s-servitor... Disp-po-posal!"

婕伊沮丧地叹了口气。“好——吧，咱们来试试别的办法吧。你说呢，亲爱的？”

"Sister Argenta, for instance..." Jae's voice becomes noticeably warmer. "She could engage the people in a prayer or tell a story about some saint or other in exchange for their queue tickets."

"Humility, acceptance, meekness... Those are the qualities that I entirely lack, shereen." Jae smiles acidly and leaves you alone with your thoughts.

又过了八个小时。队伍中的人几乎一动不动，而隔壁窗口的认证官则忙着处理沉思者中拒绝服从命令的机魂。因此，那个窗口的队伍也插进了你的队伍之中。
Another eight planetary hours go by. The queue has hardly moved — the adept in the next window was dealing with rebelling machine spirits in his cogitator, so the petitioners from that queue were diverted to the middle of yours.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

你在队伍中迎来了黄昏，又迎来了黎明。你通过大厅的窗户，观察着瓦兰修斯领不断变化的天光。夜晚平静地过去了，认证官离开了窗口，去睡觉了，机仆们替代了他们的位置。但遗憾的是，机仆并不能处理请愿者的所有请求。因此，到了晚上，队伍移动得更加缓慢。
You greeted the dusk and dawn from your place in the queue, observing the shifting rays of the Mundis Valancius through the windows of the palace. The night passed peacefully — the certification officers left for their beds and servitors took their place. Unfortunately, servitors cannot process all petitioner requests, so at night the queue moved even more slowly.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

"Wasting the Inquisition's time on this foolishness, it's simply unthinkable!" Wearied by the long wait, Heinrix is rereading confidential reports on his data-slate for the tenth time.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“又到了这个该死的地方。当我打算结婚的时候，就在这条队伍里等着。每当我的子女出生时，我都不得不在这条队伍里等着，这样他们的名字才会被记入达戈努斯的史册。而当我挚爱的妻子离世的时候，我依然在等着。”阿贝拉德垂头丧气地叹息着。
"This accursed place again. I stood in this queue when I was planning to marry. I stood in it when every son and every daughter was born, so that their names would be entered in the chronicle of Dargonus. And when my dear wife departed this mortal world, I waited again." Abelard sighs dejectedly.

今天，整个首都都在庆祝你祖先的诞辰。当初，就是米尔蒂亚斯·奥勒斯特·希恩·冯·瓦兰修斯发现了基亚瓦伽马星，在那里建立了殖民地。达戈努斯的每座巢都都在举行祈祷仪式。贵族与平民涌上街头，参加各种娱乐活动，就连德莱夫斯塔总督本人都登上了宫殿的尖塔，发表了年度演讲。内政部绝大多数仆人都加入了这场庆典，因此，今天只有一位认证官在处理各种事务。
Today the entire capital is celebrating the birthday of your ancestor — Miltiades Orest Theon von Valancius, who discovered and colonised Kiava Gamma. In every hive on Dargonus, prayer services are being held in his honour, nobles and commoners are attending fairs with amusements, and Governor Drivestem himself is giving his annual speech from the main spire of his palace. Most of the Administratum servants have joined the festivities, so today all of the windows are being served by only one certification officer.

“既然这些坏种希望被人坑骗，那我不打算阻止他们。”婕伊自鸣得意地看着躁动不安的人群。他们彼此窃窃私语着，用手里的叫号票互相指指点点。
"If these ashmags want to be tricked, I won't stop them." Jae smugly watches the agitated crowd, whispering among themselves and jabbing each other with sheaves of paper.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

队伍中再次散发出了充满活力的嗡嗡声。请愿者们互相打量着，握紧了各自的叫号票。几秒种后，你意识到，伺服头骨第三次喊出的号码，就是你的票上的号码。
The hum of activity returns to the queue. Petitioners exchange glances, clutching their paperwork. After a few seconds, you realise that the number being called out by the servo-skull for the third time is the one on your ticket.

"Do you know what gets better with time, shereen? Amasec and lovemaking. Remind me of that if I ever ask you to stand in a queue again."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

“嗯……这比我想象得要快。当然，我们确实等了一小会儿，不过有的时候，等待也是件有趣的事情。”婕伊疲惫地笑着。“只有再盖上最后一个印章，再认证一次……帝国官方贸易代表婕伊·海达利就会站在你面前了！”
"Well... That went faster than I expected. We had a little bit of a wait, of course, but at times it was actually fun." Jae smiles wearily. "One last seal. One more certification and... you will be looking at Official Trade Representative Jae Heydari!"

  • 注：出现条件：Companion

“说实话，亲爱的。我之前试图说服海因里希，让他用审讯官的玫瑰结来帮助我们脱离困境。我尽我所能地甜言蜜语、巧言令色，但他却……完全无动于衷，就像一块石头，完全不在意清风的舞蹈。或许，他会听从你的请求？”
"I'll be honest, shereen, I already tried to convince Heinrix to use his Interrogator's rosette, with sweet words and pretty songs I cajoled and wheedled. But he... remains unmoved, like a rock whipped by the winds. Perhaps he will be more amenable to a request from you?"

"Sister Argenta, for instance..." Jae's voice becomes noticeably warmer. "She could engage the people in a prayer or tell a story about some saint or other in exchange for their queue tickets."

  • 注：出现条件：Companion

"The people will be amazed if you show them your tamed xenos! They'll drop everything they're holding — including their tickets — and come to goggle at her, I guarantee it."

"We've got a servant of the Lex Imperialis on our team, and with a formidable dog to boot! Though the Proctor could probably just stare at the queue, and it would move right aside."

[看着某个看起来心地善良的人]
[Address a tender-hearted man]

婕伊循着你的目光，将手搭在某个看起来很疲惫的人肩膀上。“愿帝皇照亮你的道路，兄弟！我是婕伊，这位是{name}。咱们一起排了这么久的队，甚至可以算得上是一家人了。可不可以告诉我们，是什么原因让你来到了这座秩序的殿堂？”
Jae catches your eye and lays her hand on the shoulder of a weary-looking man. "May the Emperor illuminate your path, brother! I am Jae, and this is {name}. We've been in the queue so long already, we're all practically family now — won't you tell us what brought you to the palace of order?"

那个男人惊讶地开了口。“呃？没错，没错，愿黄金王座的光芒保佑你！我叫梅纳斯，梅纳斯·德·皮尔。我已经在这里呆了一个月了，试遍了所有办法，想到达那扇窗户，但无论什么方法都不管用。我可怜的伊莲娜，我可怜的亲生女儿。那些人把她扣留在了维博斯六号星，还对她提出了指控，你敢相信会发生这种事情吗？那些指控都是假的！我们的内政部就是这么不干人事。”说完这句话，梅纳斯赶紧捂住了嘴，惊恐地四处张望。
The man starts in surprise. "Eh? Yes, yes, light of the Throne bless you! My name is Menas. Menas de Pyrr. I have been here a month already. I've tried everything I can to get through to that window. Nothing working. My poor, poor Ilena. She's my daughter, my flesh and blood. They detained her on Vheabos VI. Charged her — can you believe it? The charges were false! That's how our Administratum operates." Menas covers his mouth and glances around fearfully.

“我有点说过头了，我真的很抱歉。那都是在瞎说，瞎说而已。我只是在想我的女儿，她被关在维博斯，被铐在矿井里。我可怜的伊莲娜！她就像鲜花一样娇嫩。她的肺不好，你懂的吧？她总是咳嗽，可她现在却被关在了矿井里？要呼吸那么多灰尘和泥土？她受不了，她绝对受不了！她本该两年前就无罪释放了，可她依然被关在里面，就因为我没弄到认证和印章，你敢相信吗？这么长时间过去了……而我却站在这里，一直在等着。算了，这已经不重要了。总之，按照这个队伍现在的速度，恐怕我们至少要等上十个周期，才能等到叫号。”
"I've said too much. I do apologise — it's my nerves. My nerves. I just keep thinking about her there on Vheabos, shackled down in the mines. My poor, poor Ilena! As delicate as a flower, she is. She's got weak lungs, you understand? Always coughing. And her now down the mines? All that dust and muck? She won't cope with it, she won't! She was acquitted two years ago. But to get the papers certified, and the seal? So much time has passed... And now here I am, standing, waiting. It doesn't matter. At the rate this queue's moving, it'll be ten cycles or more before our numbers come up."

那个男人惊讶地开了口。“呃？没错，没错，愿黄金王座的光芒保佑你！我叫梅纳斯，梅纳斯·德·皮尔。我已经在这里呆了一个月了，试遍了所有办法，想到达那扇窗户，但无论什么方法都不管用。我可怜的伊莲娜，我可怜的亲生女儿。那些人把她扣留在了维博斯六号星，还对她提出了指控，你敢相信会发生这种事情吗？那些指控都是假的！我们的内政部就是这么不干人事。”说完这句话，梅纳斯赶紧捂住了嘴，惊恐地四处张望。
The man starts in surprise. "Eh? Yes, yes, light of the Throne bless you! My name is Menas. Menas de Pyrr. I have been here a month already. I've tried everything I can to get through to that window. Nothing working. My poor, poor Ilena. She's my daughter, my flesh and blood. They detained her on Vheabos VI. Charged her — can you believe it? The charges were false! That's how our Administratum operates." Menas covers his mouth and glances around fearfully.

“我有点说过头了，我真的很抱歉。那都是在瞎说，瞎说而已。我只是在想我的女儿，她被关在维博斯，被铐在矿井里。我可怜的伊莲娜！她就像鲜花一样娇嫩。她的肺不好，你懂的吧？她总是咳嗽，可她现在却被关在了矿井里？要呼吸那么多灰尘和泥土？她受不了，她绝对受不了！她本该两年前就无罪释放了，可她依然被关在里面，就因为我没弄到认证和印章，你敢相信吗？这么长时间过去了……而我却站在这里，一直在等着。算了，这已经不重要了。总之，按照这个队伍现在的速度，恐怕我们至少要等上十个周期，才能等到叫号。”
"I've said too much. I do apologise — it's my nerves. My nerves. I just keep thinking about her there on Vheabos, shackled down in the mines. My poor, poor Ilena! As delicate as a flower, she is. She's got weak lungs, you understand? Always coughing. And her now down the mines? All that dust and muck? She won't cope with it, she won't! She was acquitted two years ago. But to get the papers certified, and the seal? So much time has passed... And now here I am, standing, waiting. It doesn't matter. At the rate this queue's moving, it'll be ten cycles or more before our numbers come up."

年轻人考虑几分钟之后，撕烂了手中的申请单。“您说得没错，把妓女与酒鬼从死亡的边缘拖回来，并不是什么光彩的事情。这么说来，自我堕落的贵族也同样没有拯救的价值。”他冷冷地看着他的母亲。“我生来就是为了拯救别人的生命。现在看来，恐怕没有比帝国卫队更适合我的地方了。”
The young man considers this for a few minutes, and then rips up his piece of paper. "You are right. There is no honour in dragging back trollops and drunks from the edge of death. Or self-indulgent nobles, for that matter." He looks coldly at his mother. "I was born to save lives. And there is no better place to do that than in the Imperial Guard."

“不，斯特福，我不是这个意思——住手！求求你了！好好考虑考虑吧！”
"No, Steffo, that's not what I— stop! Please! Think about this!"

“你处理事务的方式很有趣，亲爱的。我会牢记这一点的。”婕伊目视着年轻的请愿者离开，精明的双眼中闪烁着饶有兴致的光芒。
"You have an interesting way of doing business, shereen. I'll keep that in mind." Jae's shrewd eyes are alight with interest as she watches the young petitioner leave.

在短暂的停顿之后，一位破衣烂衫的驼背老人朝你走了过来。这个老人的牙齿已经掉光。他张开口，呼出一团恶臭。断断续续地说了四个字：“重……获……新生……”
After allowing you a brief pause, a hunched ragamuffin approaches you. The old man's toothless mouth breathes out a putrefying cloud of air as he speaks only three words: "Death-th-th... f-f-for life..."

婕伊的目光越过了他的肩膀，看着他手上皱巴巴的表格。“你……是来请求进行遗体捐赠的吗？这样一来，你的器官就可以作为你的遗产，归你的孙女所有，对吗？但她恐怕不会想要你破破烂烂的身体，老家伙……”
Jae peers over the man's shoulder to read his crumpled form. "You... are here to request mortification, so that your organs go to your granddaughter as an inheritance? She will hardly want your worn-out body parts, old-timer..."

这个衣衫褴褛的人摇了摇头，满是皱纹的手遮住了他的脸。“机仆……配件！”
The ragged man shakes his head and covers his face with his wrinkled hands. "S-s-servitor... Disp-po-posal!"

"In the name of House von Valancius, I hereby make your fiancée a lady of the court. And release her from any obligations thereto."

Most of the Administratum servants have joined the festivities, so today all of the windows are being served by only one certification officer.

“噢，舰长大人，这个地方充斥着褪了色的丑陋污点！我感到头晕目眩……”卡西娅用厚厚的披肩遮住了双眼。“事实证明，帝国内政部的殿堂就像那些仆人写出来的作品一样，令人失望不已。”
"Oh, Lord Captain, this place teems with hideous stains of washed-out colours! It makes my head spin..." Cassia covers her eyes with a thick shawl. "The Palace of the Adeptus Administratum has proved to be just as depressing as the published works of its servants."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

今天，整个首都都在庆祝你祖先的诞辰。当初，就是米尔蒂亚斯·奥勒斯特·希恩·冯·瓦兰修斯发现了基亚瓦伽马星，在那里建立了殖民地。达戈努斯的每座巢都都在举行祈祷仪式。贵族与平民涌上街头，参加各种娱乐活动，就连德莱夫斯塔总督本人都登上了宫殿的尖塔，发表了年度演讲。内政部绝大多数仆人都加入了这场庆典，因此，今天只有一位认证官在处理各种事务。
Today the entire capital is celebrating the birthday of your ancestor — Miltiades Orest Theon von Valancius, who discovered and colonised Kiava Gamma. In every hive on Dargonus, prayer services are being held in his honour, nobles and commoners are attending fairs with amusements, and Governor Drivestem himself is giving his annual speech from the main spire of his palace. Most of the Administratum servants have joined the festivities, so today all of the windows are being served by only one certification officer.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“正在记录毫无建设性，浪费时间资源的行为。建议解决方案：返回初始任务。”
"Unconstructive expenditure of temporal resources recorded. Recommended resolution: return to initial mission."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“混沌大敌正在整个科罗努斯扩区策划阴谋，准备对付神皇的追随者，可我们却不得不在这里等待一纸凭证！”阿洁塔愤怒地瞪着婕伊。“而且，这么做还不是为了帝国的利益，不是！而是为了满足某个异端分子的异想天开！”
"The Archenemy is plotting against His servants throughout the Expanse, and we are forced to wait here for a piece of paper to be certified!" Argenta tosses a furious look at Jae. "And not for the good of the Imperium, no, but to satisfy the whim of a heretic!"

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

“舰长大人，这个地方实在是太无聊了，就连另一边的敲门声都没有了。那些家伙意识到这里没有任何有趣的事情，甚至都不再窃窃私语了！咱们就不能回到船上去吗？”
"Lord Captain, this place is so dull there's not even any knocking on the other side of the door — all the whispers died down when they realised nothing interesting was going to happen! Can't we go back to the ship?"

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

索罗蒙仿佛石像一样，面无表情地站在一大群卑微的请愿者之中，身躯一动不动，目光不停地扫视着周围。
Solomorne stands impassively like a stone column amidst the throng of lowly petitioners, unmoving except for his eyes, which sweep the perimeter like a guard-visor.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

接下来的八个小时，也同样是出乎意料地平静。没有发生任何不寻常的事情，所有的认证官都在各自的窗口接待请愿者。你甚至已经渐渐开始习惯这个地方的声音与气味了。
The next eight hours pass surprisingly peacefully — nothing unusual happens, all the certification officers are at their windows and are accepting petitioners, and you have even started growing accustomed to the sounds and smells of this place.

“亲爱的……你真是个圣人，我以前有没有这么说过？你绝对是个圣人，因为你的耐心是如此热忱，又是如此毫无意义，我根本看不出来你为什么要这么做。我们就不能抓紧时间吗？”
"Shereen... You're a saint, have I told you that before? You must be, because I don't see any other reason why you would show such fervent but senseless patience. Can't we hurry things along?"

“好吧，亲爱的。或许你这次会失去耐心，打算让事情进行得快一些？”
"Well, shereen, maybe this time you will lose patience with being patient and decide to move things along a teensy bit faster?"

又过了八个小时。队伍中的人几乎一动不动，而隔壁窗口的认证官则忙着处理沉思者中拒绝服从命令的机魂。因此，那个窗口的队伍也插进了你的队伍之中。
Another eight planetary hours go by. The queue has hardly moved — the adept in the next window was dealing with rebelling machine spirits in his cogitator, so the petitioners from that queue were diverted to the middle of yours.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

你在队伍中迎来了黄昏，又迎来了黎明。你通过大厅的窗户，观察着瓦兰修斯领不断变化的天光。夜晚平静地过去了，认证官离开了窗口，去睡觉了，机仆们替代了他们的位置。但遗憾的是，机仆并不能处理请愿者的所有请求。因此，到了晚上，队伍移动得更加缓慢。
You greeted the dusk and dawn from your place in the queue, observing the shifting rays of the Mundis Valancius through the windows of the palace. The night passed peacefully — the certification officers left for their beds and servitors took their place. Unfortunately, servitors cannot process all petitioner requests, so at night the queue moved even more slowly.

I have already found our first vict— ah, the compassionate citizen who is standing fifty places ahead of us in the queue. And also... you have the power to solve the problems of some petitioners, removing their need to visit a coveted window. Jae catches your eye and lays her hand on the shoulder of a weary-looking man. "May the Emperor illuminate your path, brother! I am Jae, and this is {name}. We've been in the queue so long already, we're all practically family now — won't you tell us what brought you to the palace of order?"

那个男人惊讶地开了口。“呃？没错，没错，愿黄金王座的光芒保佑你！我叫梅纳斯，梅纳斯·德·皮尔。我已经在这里呆了一个月了，试遍了所有办法，想到达那扇窗户，但无论什么方法都不管用。我可怜的伊莲娜，我可怜的亲生女儿。那些人把她扣留在了维博斯六号星，还对她提出了指控，你敢相信会发生这种事情吗？那些指控都是假的！我们的内政部就是这么不干人事。”说完这句话，梅纳斯赶紧捂住了嘴，惊恐地四处张望。
The man starts in surprise. "Eh? Yes, yes, light of the Throne bless you! My name is Menas. Menas de Pyrr. I have been here a month already. I've tried everything I can to get through to that window. Nothing working. My poor, poor Ilena. She's my daughter, my flesh and blood. They detained her on Vheabos VI. Charged her — can you believe it? The charges were false! That's how our Administratum operates." Menas covers his mouth and glances around fearfully.

“我有点说过头了，我真的很抱歉。那都是在瞎说，瞎说而已。我只是在想我的女儿，她被关在维博斯，被铐在矿井里。我可怜的伊莲娜！她就像鲜花一样娇嫩。她的肺不好，你懂的吧？她总是咳嗽，可她现在却被关在了矿井里？要呼吸那么多灰尘和泥土？她受不了，她绝对受不了！她本该两年前就无罪释放了，可她依然被关在里面，就因为我没弄到认证和印章，你敢相信吗？这么长时间过去了……而我却站在这里，一直在等着。算了，这已经不重要了。总之，按照这个队伍现在的速度，恐怕我们至少要等上十个周期，才能等到叫号。”
"I've said too much. I do apologise — it's my nerves. My nerves. I just keep thinking about her there on Vheabos, shackled down in the mines. My poor, poor Ilena! As delicate as a flower, she is. She's got weak lungs, you understand? Always coughing. And her now down the mines? All that dust and muck? She won't cope with it, she won't! She was acquitted two years ago. But to get the papers certified, and the seal? So much time has passed... And now here I am, standing, waiting. It doesn't matter. At the rate this queue's moving, it'll be ten cycles or more before our numbers come up."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

队伍中再次散发出了充满活力的嗡嗡声。请愿者们互相打量着，握紧了各自的叫号票。几秒种后，你意识到，伺服头骨第三次喊出的号码，就是你的票上的号码。
The hum of activity returns to the queue. Petitioners exchange glances, clutching their paperwork. After a few seconds, you realise that the number being called out by the servo-skull for the third time is the one on your ticket.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

“噢，至高无上的神皇啊，感谢你赐予行商浪人神圣的授状与特权！我对天发誓，如果我们当时再多等一分钟，我肯定会开枪打人了！”
"O, Exalted One, thank you for granting the Rogue Trader his/her sacred Warrant and all its privileges! If we had had to wait a minute longer, heaven be my witness, I would have shot someone!"

"Do you know what gets better with time, shereen? Amasec and lovemaking. Remind me of that if I ever ask you to stand in a queue again."

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

又过了八个小时。队伍中的人几乎一动不动，而隔壁窗口的认证官则忙着处理沉思者中拒绝服从命令的机魂。因此，那个窗口的队伍也插进了你的队伍之中。
Another eight planetary hours go by. The queue has hardly moved — the adept in the next window was dealing with rebelling machine spirits in his cogitator, so the petitioners from that queue were diverted to the middle of yours.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag

你在队伍中迎来了黄昏，又迎来了黎明。你通过大厅的窗户，观察着瓦兰修斯领不断变化的天光。夜晚平静地过去了，认证官离开了窗口，去睡觉了，机仆们替代了他们的位置。但遗憾的是，机仆并不能处理请愿者的所有请求。因此，到了晚上，队伍移动得更加缓慢。
You greeted the dusk and dawn from your place in the queue, observing the shifting rays of the Mundis Valancius through the windows of the palace. The night passed peacefully — the certification officers left for their beds and servitors took their place. Unfortunately, servitors cannot process all petitioner requests, so at night the queue moved even more slowly.

  • 注：出现条件：Flag、Companion

"Wasting the Inquisition's time on this foolishness, it's simply unthinkable!" Wearied by the long wait, Heinrix is rereading confidential reports on his data-slate for the tenth time.

"This accursed place again. I stood in this queue when I was planning to marry. I stood in it when every son and every daughter was born, so that their names would be entered in the chronicle of Dargonus. And when my dear wife departed this mortal world, I waited again." Abelard sighs dejectedly.

Today the entire capital is celebrating the birthday of your ancestor — Miltiades Orest Theon von Valancius, who discovered and colonised Kiava Gamma. In every hive on Dargonus, prayer services are being held in his honour, nobles and commoners are attending fairs with amusements, and Governor Drivestem himself is giving his annual speech from the main spire of his palace. Most of the Administratum servants have joined the festivities, so today all of the windows are being served by only one certification officer.

"Frighten the people. These worms should bow down in terror before their master/mistress and let us through."

"As you wish, Your Lordship/Ladyship," Jae says in a deliberately deferential tone and makes her way to the centre of the room.

"Hem-ahem. Attention, all! Before you is His Lordship/Her Ladyship {name} von Valancius, Rogue Trader and anointed sovereign of this world! Bow your unworthy heads and give your master/mistress his/her rightful place in the queue!"

"We shall solve the problems of the common people."

"A wise decision, shereen! Cold Traders always say: if you can solve a problem with hard cash, then that's just the cost of doing business!"

婕伊意有所指地看了你一眼，之后稍稍退了一步。“噢，至高无上的神皇在上，莫非今天是我的幸运日吗？我再也不用在这个大厅里日夜等候了，因为冯·瓦兰修斯家族这位善良的大人/女士是所有穷苦之人的庇护主，他/她已经帮我解决了我的问题！”
Jae gives you a conspiratorial wink and backs away slightly. "O Exalted One, could today be my lucky day? No longer will I have to stand in this hall, waiting day and night for my turn to come, for this kind lord/lady of House von Valancius is a benefactor of the downtrodden, and he/she has solved my problem!"

“尊敬的大人/女士，请您可怜可怜我这个年轻人吧！只要你能帮忙解决我的问题，我向帝皇发誓，我愿意把我的一切都献给您！”
"Esteemed lord/lady, take pity on this poor youth as well! I will give you everything I have, I swear before the Emperor! Only help me solve my problem."

“我们才不需要你献出一切呢，可怜虫。只要把你的位置让给我们就行了。”
"We do not need everything, poor wretch. Only your place in the queue."

"You do not need to tell me twice, shereen. All is fair in love and bureaucracy..."

"If these ashmags want to be tricked, I won't stop them." Jae smugly watches the agitated crowd, whispering among themselves and jabbing each other with sheaves of paper.

[看着某个看起来心地善良的人]
[Address a tender-hearted man]

婕伊循着你的目光，将手搭在某个看起来很疲惫的人肩膀上。“愿帝皇照亮你的道路，兄弟！我是婕伊，这位是{name}。咱们一起排了这么久的队，甚至可以算得上是一家人了。可不可以告诉我们，是什么原因让你来到了这座秩序的殿堂？”
Jae catches your eye and lays her hand on the shoulder of a weary-looking man. "May the Emperor illuminate your path, brother! I am Jae, and this is {name}. We've been in the queue so long already, we're all practically family now — won't you tell us what brought you to the palace of order?"

那个男人惊讶地开了口。“呃？没错，没错，愿黄金王座的光芒保佑你！我叫梅纳斯，梅纳斯·德·皮尔。我已经在这里呆了一个月了，试遍了所有办法，想到达那扇窗户，但无论什么方法都不管用。我可怜的伊莲娜，我可怜的亲生女儿。那些人把她扣留在了维博斯六号星，还对她提出了指控，你敢相信会发生这种事情吗？那些指控都是假的！我们的内政部就是这么不干人事。”说完这句话，梅纳斯赶紧捂住了嘴，惊恐地四处张望。
The man starts in surprise. "Eh? Yes, yes, light of the Throne bless you! My name is Menas. Menas de Pyrr. I have been here a month already. I've tried everything I can to get through to that window. Nothing working. My poor, poor Ilena. She's my daughter, my flesh and blood. They detained her on Vheabos VI. Charged her — can you believe it? The charges were false! That's how our Administratum operates." Menas covers his mouth and glances around fearfully.

“我有点说过头了，我真的很抱歉。那都是在瞎说，瞎说而已。我只是在想我的女儿，她被关在维博斯，被铐在矿井里。我可怜的伊莲娜！她就像鲜花一样娇嫩。她的肺不好，你懂的吧？她总是咳嗽，可她现在却被关在了矿井里？要呼吸那么多灰尘和泥土？她受不了，她绝对受不了！她本该两年前就无罪释放了，可她依然被关在里面，就因为我没弄到认证和印章，你敢相信吗？这么长时间过去了……而我却站在这里，一直在等着。算了，这已经不重要了。总之，按照这个队伍现在的速度，恐怕我们至少要等上十个周期，才能等到叫号。”
"I've said too much. I do apologise — it's my nerves. My nerves. I just keep thinking about her there on Vheabos, shackled down in the mines. My poor, poor Ilena! As delicate as a flower, she is. She's got weak lungs, you understand? Always coughing. And her now down the mines? All that dust and muck? She won't cope with it, she won't! She was acquitted two years ago. But to get the papers certified, and the seal? So much time has passed... And now here I am, standing, waiting. It doesn't matter. At the rate this queue's moving, it'll be ten cycles or more before our numbers come up."

"I want to consider everything again."

"Of course, shereen. Our number in the queue is..." Jae checks the ticket. "O, Exalted One, I wish I hadn't looked. We are definitely not going anywhere soon, shereen. You need to make a decision."
